TI CHARACTERISTICS OF SI DOPED GAAS GROWN ON (111)A, B AND (100) SUBSTRATES
   BY MBE IN RELATION TO LATTICE LOCATION OF SI
SO INSTITUTE OF PHYSICS CONFERENCE SERIES <D>
LA English
DT Article
AB Si-doped GaAs grown on (111)A, B and (100) oriented substrates by MBE was characterized by C-V, Hall, SIMS, photoluminescence, Raman scattering and XFR measurements.  Above [Si] approximately 6 x 10(18) cm-3 the electron concentration of (111)B layers saturates and then decreases, and deep PL band appears as in the case of (100) growth, where these phenomena have been explained by the formation of Si(Ga)-complexes.  On the contrary, for (111)A growth, doped Si atoms occupy As sites and act as acceptors with no deep level emission up to [Si] approximately 6 x 10(19)cm-3.  At higher doping concentration, Si starts to occupy Ga sites resulting in the saturation of carrier density by autocompensation mechanism and, at much higher concentration, the formation of Si(Ga)-complexes takes place.

TI RAMAN-SCATTERING DEPTH PROFILE OF MBE GROWN ALXGA1-XAS/GAAS AND GAAS/SI
SO INSTITUTE OF PHYSICS CONFERENCE SERIES <D>
LA English
DT Article
ID INTERFACE; SUBSTRATE; STRESS; LAYER
AB The residual stress in various heterostructures has been characterized by micro-Raman spectroscopy.  In a GaAs/Si structure, the TO phonon peak position shifts to lower frequency by about 0.9 cm-1.  This correspond to tensile stress of about 4.5 x 10(9) dyn/cm2.  On the other hand, a very large peak shift of Raman spectra in the Al(x)Ga(1-x)As/GaAs system has been found.  Residual stress of this system is estimated to be about 2.0 approximately 15 x 10(9) dyn/cm2 in a compressive mode.

TI SPECIFIC LATTICE SITES AND DISPLACEMENT OF SI ATOMS HEAVILY IMPLANTED
   INTO GAAS BY ION-CHANNELING METHOD
SO INSTITUTE OF PHYSICS CONFERENCE SERIES <D>
LA English
DT Article
ID LOCATION; CRYSTALS
AB In order to clarify the saturation mechanism of carrier concentration in heavily Si implanted GaAs crystals, we have carried out ion-channeling experiments with special techniques (asymmetry effects and temperature dependence of dechanneling fractions).  From the experiment on asymmetry, it is found that the substitutional Si atoms located in Ga sites prevail over those in As sites.  Moreover, from the experiment on temperature dependence, the displacement of Si atoms is estimated to be approximately 0.  1-angstrom from the ideal lattice site.  Therefore, it is concluded that the displacement of donor atoms is most responsible for the saturation.

TI EXAFS AND XANES STUDY ON SPINEL STRUCTURE MATERIALS AND THEIR
   APPLICATION TO HUMIDITY SENSOR
SO JOURNAL DE PHYSIQUE
LA English
DT Article
AB The deterioration mechanism of the humidity sensors were investigated by Fe K-EXAFS and XANES. The humidity sensors were composed of spinel structure materials, Zn0.98Na0.02Fe2O4 and Mg0.98Na0.02Fe2O4. The former is excellent in durability, while the latter is poor. It was suggested that the deterioration of Mg0.98Na0.02Fe2O4 is attributable to the movement of Fe atoms. It was shown that a laboratory scale equipment is extremely useful tool to study not only the atomic radial distribution, but also the coordination geometry around excited atoms.
